{"nick":"tamarind","reason":"\"Leaving\"","date":"2018-07-10T10:32:57.267Z","type":"part"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"that is, the code in each module is isolated, and doesn't expose anything globally","date":"2018-07-10T10:33:03.358Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"if you want to expose anything from a module, you need to explicitly export it; and in the module in which you want to *use* it, you need to require the module you want to use","date":"2018-07-10T10:33:27.847Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"this provides a bunch of technical benefits (most notably it prevents conflicts between modules), but it does mean that it doesn't work like includes","date":"2018-07-10T10:33:47.365Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"wickstjo","message":"right","date":"2018-07-10T10:34:07.080Z","type":"message"}
